slovak spanish swedish turkish updated 1 january 2023 this applicant privacy notice privacy notice describes how honeywell international inc and its affiliates collectively honeywell us or we process your personal information when you join our talent community search or apply for a job and submit personal information to us via our portal websites or other recruitment mediums whether online or offline the services we are the controllers of your personal information for the purposes of applicable data protection laws please note that if you are already a honeywell employee you can also refer to the honeywell global data privacy policy and the employee privacy notice where one exists for your jurisdiction the aim of this privacy notice is to give you more detailed information about our processing of your personal information in relation to your application personal information we collect to process your application we ask you to provide the personal information about yourself for example when you apply for a particular job vacancy through our websiteportal or in case that you already are a honeywell employee during your employment relationship all information is provided on a voluntary basis and you determine the extent of information you provide to honeywell please bear in mind that some information may be necessary to complete an evaluation of your application and if it is not provided our ability to consider you as a candidate may be limited i personal information we may collect the following personal information about you personal details and contact information including email address telephone numbers and photograph professional and educational information related to your occupation such as your current or previous employers your job title or other information about the organization with which you are affiliated you may also provide your cvresume and information about your qualifications or your education such as your degrees fields of study the institutions youve attended languages professional memberships certifications details on performance management ratings and compensation career preferences eg shortterm and longterm goals willingness to relocate date available to relocate and location preferences personal information derived from your participation in our recruitment process such as for example those obtained during interviews the emails we exchange with you regarding your application or the conversations we have with you through our online chatbot audio and visual information such as your voice and likeness as captured in photographs video or audio recordings if you participate in a phone or video interview or if you visit our offices any other personal information that you voluntarily choose to provide to us ii sensitive personal information we may also collect special categories of personal information about you also known as special categories of personal information where we have a legal obligation to do so or the information is relevant to your future working environment at honeywell or for the future provision of employment benefits or with your explicit consent such as governmentissued identification number such as a social security number demographic information which may include information about protected classifications such as your age gender race disabilities sexual orientation marital status or veteran status health information for example to accommodate any disability you may have or dietary restrictions information relating to a persons political opinions or religious beliefs or trade union membership information about an individuals criminal offences or convictions as well as any other information deemed sensitive under applicable data protection laws where permitted by law and to the extent applicable honeywell may also need to carry out background andor criminal checks to determine your suitability for an open position or opportunity at honeywell we do not require you to provide us with sensitive personal information unless it is necessary for the purposes of carrying out our regulatory obligations eg for equal opportunity monitoring or unless you have provided your explicit consent except to the extent required by law the provision of this information will be entirely voluntary honeywell is committed to a true inclusive and diverse workforce by providing us with your equal opportunity data you allow us to better understand our employee profile in terms of equal opportunities data and the action we need to take to attract promote and retain a diverse workforce regardless of age disability gender race religious or philosophical beliefs and sexual orientation iii personal information we collect automatically from you we may automatically collect certain information from you about your visit to our websites using cookies and other similar tracking technologies for further information about the cookies we use on the website through which you submit your application please read our cookie notice sources of personal information we may collect your personal information directly from you or indirectly from third parties who are lawfully entitled to share your information with us such as employment agencies backgroundemployment check or identity verification service providers recruitment agencies for example when a recruitment agency identifies you as a potential candidate publicly available information about you from sites such as linkedin or your current employers website you may also choose to provide us with access to certain personal information stored by third parties for example linkedin twitter google or facebook by authorizing honeywell to have access to this information you agree that we may collect store and use this information in accordance with this privacy notice by reference or word of mouth for example through a referral from a current or former employee for referrals the person who is referring you will be responsible for obtaining your consent to provide us with your personal information purposes for which personal information is used we use your personal information for the following purposes to evaluate your application and make hiring decisions communicate with you and to inform you about the recruitment andor your applications or any other required communications comply with applicable legal and regulatory requirements and in order for us to establish exercise or defend a legal claim employment and corporate management for example establish a basic employment record if you are hired to carry out aggregated reports analysis regarding candidates activity data eg career site traffic candidate funnel source of hire recruiting campaign success for honeywell employees only to automatically exclude you from being proactively suggested for consideration to recruiters for a job opportunity and are not eligible for consideration per your current hpd 9block rating which will never be revealed to anyone outside honeywell however you will always be able to directly apply for any job opportunity available and your specific situation will be considered by a recruiter only where you are a resident of the united states to send you communications via sms specifically i 11 sms communications in connection with your application to a particular job vacancy andor ii subject to your express consent sms campaign communications about employment opportunities job affairs and application updates you will be able to opt out andor revoke your consent for receiving the abovementioned communications following the instructions given in your profile if you are offered and accept employment with honeywell the information collected during the application and recruitment process will become part of your employment record automated processing and profiling subject to your express consent which you voluntarily provide when joining our talent community or when checking the appropriate consent box during the application process we conduct profiling to evaluate your suitability for particular job opportunities this involves using a matching algorithm that is able to evaluate your employment profile and predict your eligibility for a particular job opportunity we carry out this automated processing for the purposes of helping recruiters match candidates profiles to job opportunities by suggesting candidates for consideration for a specific job opportunity and sending personalized job recommendations to you based on your profile andor preferences or other information that may be of interest for you such as honeywell news webinars and events please note that based on this profiling you may not be considered for certain job opportunities unless you have applied for them directly we do not make hiring decisions based solely on automated decisionmaking processes andor profiling your personal information will be subjected to humanmade decisions as the ultimate hiring decision will be made by the recruiters or hiring manager the legal bases for processing your personal information certain jurisdictions require honeywell to have a legal basis for processing your personal information where applicable law requires us to justify our processing activities our legal basis for collecting and using your personal information as described in this privacy notice will depend on the personal information concerned and the specific context in which we collect it consent in general we will normally collect personal information from you where we have your consent to do so and where we need your personal information to process your application by accessing our websiteportal joining our talent community or applying for one of our job positions you provide your consent to honeywell to collect and further process the personal information described above for the purposes described in this privacy notice you may withdraw your consent at any time by making submitting a request through our data subject request portal at httpswwwhoneywellcomenusprivacystatement or sending us an email to honeywellprivacyhoneywellcom legitimate interests in honeywells legitimate interests namely the recruitment selection evaluation and appointment of new employees and the management and administration of the recruitment and the hr process to the extent our legitimate interests are not overridden by your fundamental rights and freedoms legal obligations compliance with honeywells legal obligations where employment law or other laws require the processing of your personal information for example to the extent the law requires the monitoring equality of opportunity and diversity vital interests we may also need your personal information to protect your vital interests for example health and safety reasons if you attend an interview at our site if you have any questions about or need further information concerning the legal basis on which we collect and use your personal information please send an email to honeywellprivacyhoneywellcom who we share your personal information with honeywell will only share your personal information with third parties under the following circumstances honeywell group entities we may share your personal information with other group entities located in jurisdictions around the world for evaluating your profile and consideration for any recruitment opportunities at a group level service providers we may specifically share your personal information with third party service providers that perform specific services on our behalf for example recruitment and outsourcing staffing providers and analytics providers such third parties may vary depending on your country and will change from time to time but may include phenom people inc cornerstone ondemand inc and their respective thirdparty providers honeywell employees if you are already a honeywell employee please note that some sections on your profile are public and therefore visible to all honeywell employees specifically your name title photograph skills interest areas work experience and education however such sections are editable and you will be able to choose which information about you is shown in your profile please note that the career goals relocations and profile status open to new opportunities sections will not be public and therefore not visible to all honeywell employees only to honeywells talent team other third parties honeywell may share your personal information with any competent law enforcement body regulator government agency court or third party where we believe the disclosure is necessary under applicable law or in the goodfaith belief that such action is necessary to exercise establish or defend our legal rights or to protect your vital interests or those of another person we may also share your personal information with others with your consent or at your direction eg a referee or professional association international transfers of personal information honeywell is a global organization and your personal information may be transferred to held stored or used across various locations worldwide such as the us and india this means that when we collect your personal information it may be processed in countries that may have data protection laws that are different to the laws of your country however honeywell will always take reasonable steps to protect your privacy and to provide a level of protection of personal information that is comparable to that of your country of residence which include implementing the european commissions standard contractual clauses which may be found at the commissions website at httpseceuropaeu retention we will retain your personal information for as long as necessary in connection with the purposes described in this privacy notice and in accordance with honeywells record retention schedule or as required by applicable law your rights depending on applicable law you may have certain rights with respect to your personal information if you are a californian resident please refer to additional information for california residents below you may have the right to access correct update or request deletion of your personal information you can object to the processing of your personal information ask us to restrict processing of your personal information or request portability of your personal information you may have the right not to have a decision made about you that is based solely on automated processing including profiling if that decision produces legal effects about you or significantly affects you honeywell does not as part of its recruitment process make solely automated decisions about candidates similarly if we have collected and process your personal information with your consent then you can withdraw your consent at any time withdrawing your consent will not affect the lawfulness of any processing we conducted prior to your withdrawal nor will it affect processing of your personal information conducted in reliance on lawful processing grounds other than consent and you have the right to complain to a data protection authority about our collection and use of your personal information we will facilitate your exercise of the rights that apply to you in accordance with applicable law to exercise any of your rights relating to your personal information please contact us through hr help or the data subject request form found at httpswwwhoneywellcomenusprivacystatement or send an email to honeywellprivacyhoneywellcom additional information for california residents if you are a resident of the state of california this section supplements honeywells applicant privacy httpswwwhoneywellcomenusprivacystatement oppdatert 1 januar 2023 denne personvernerklringen for skere personvernerklringen beskriver hvordan honeywell international inc og dets tilknyttede selskaper samlet kalt honeywell oss eller vi behandler personopplysningene dine nr du blir medlem av talent community sker eller sker p en jobb og sender inn personopplysninger til oss via vr portal vre nettsteder eller andre rekrutteringsmedier enten online eller offline tjenestene vi er behandlingsansvarlige for personopplysningene dine i henhold til gjeldende personvernlovgivning vr oppmerksom p at hvis du allerede er ansatt hos honeywell kan du ogs lese honeywells globale retningslinjer for personvern og personvernerklringen for ansatte der det finnes en slik for din jurisdiksjon formlet med denne personvernerklringen er gi deg mer detaljert informasjon om hvordan vi behandler personopplysningene dine i forbindelse med sknaden din personopplysninger vi samler inn for kunne behandle sknaden din ber vi deg om oppgi personopplysninger om deg selv for eksempel nr du sker p en bestemt ledig stilling via nettstedetportalen vr eller hvis du allerede er ansatt hos honeywell i lpet av ditt ansettelsesforhold all informasjon gis p frivillig basis og du bestemmer selv hvor mye informasjon du gir til honeywell vr oppmerksom p at enkelte opplysninger kan vre ndvendige for kunne vurdere sknaden din og hvis du ikke oppgir disse kan det begrense vr mulighet til vurdere deg som kandidat i personlig informasjon vi kan samle inn flgende personopplysninger om deg personopplysninger og kontaktinformasjon inkludert epostadresse telefonnummer og bilde yrkes og utdanningsinformasjon knyttet til yrket ditt for eksempel nvrende eller tidligere arbeidsgivere stillingstittel eller annen informasjon om organisasjonen du er tilknyttet du kan ogs oppgi cv og informasjon om kvalifikasjonene eller utdanningen din for eksempel grader studieretninger hvilke institusjoner du har gtt p sprk aviso de privacidade descreve a forma como a honeywell international inc e as suas filiais coletivamente honeywell ns ou nosso processam as suas informaes pessoais quando se junta nossa comunidade de talentos procura ou se candidata a um emprego e nos envia informaes pessoais atravs do nosso portal websites ou outros meios de recrutamento quer online quer offline os servios somos os responsveis pelo tratamento das suas informaes pessoais para efeitos das leis de proteo de dados aplicveis tenha em ateno que se j for funcionrio da honeywell tambm pode consultar a poltica global de privacidade de dados da honeywell e o aviso de privacidade do funcionrio caso exista um para a sua jurisdio o objetivo do presente aviso de privacidade fornecerlhe informaes mais detalhadas sobre o processamento das suas informaes pessoais relativamente sua candidatura informaes pessoais que recolhemos para processar a sua candidatura pedimoslhe que fornea informaes pessoais sobre si por exemplo quando se candidata a uma determinada vaga de emprego atravs do nosso websiteportal ou no caso de j ser funcionrio da honeywell durante a sua relao laboral todas as informaes so fornecidas numa base voluntria e o utilizador determina a extenso das informaes que fornece honeywell tenha em conta que algumas informaes podem ser necessrias para completar a avaliao da sua candidatura e que se no forem fornecidas a nossa capacidade de o considerar como candidato pode ser limitada i informaes pessoais podemos recolher as seguintes informaes pessoais sobre o utilizador dados pessoais e informaes de contacto incluindo endereo de correio eletrnico nmeros de telefone e fotografia informaes profissionais e educativas relacionadas com a sua ocupao tais como os seus empregadores actuais ou anteriores o seu cargo ou outras informaes sobre a organizao a que est associado pode tambm fornecer o seu cvcurrculo e informaes sobre as suas qualificaes ou formao tais como os seus diplomas reas de estudo instituies que frequentou lnguas associaes profissionais certificaes pormenores sobre classificaes de gesto do desempenho e remunerao preferncias de carreira por exemplo objectivos a curto e a longo prazo vontade de mudar de residncia data disponvel para mudar de residncia e preferncias de localizao informaes pessoais derivadas da sua participao no nosso processo de recrutamento como por exemplo as obtidas durante as entrevistas os emails que trocamos consigo relativamente sua candidatura ou as conversas que temos consigo atravs do nosso chatbot online informaes udio e visuais tais como a sua voz e imagem captadas em fotografias gravaes de vdeo ou udio se participar numa entrevista por telefone ou vdeo ou se visitar os nossos escritrios quaisquer outras informaes pessoais que o utilizador opte voluntariamente por nos fornecer ii informaes pessoais sensveis podemos tambm recolher categorias especiais de informaes pessoais sobre o utilizador tambm conhecidas como categorias especiais de informaes pessoais quando tivermos a obrigao legal de o fazer ou quando as informaes so relevantes para o seu futuro ambiente de trabalho na honeywell ou para a futura prestao de benefcios laborais ou com o seu consentimento explcito tais como governmentissued identification number such as a social security number demographic information which may include information about protected classifications such as your age gender race disabilities sexual orientation marital status or veteran status nmero de identificao emitido pelo governo como um nmero de segurana social informaes demogrficas que podem incluir informaes sobre classificaes protegidas tais como a sua idade sexo raa incapacidades orientao sexual estado civil ou estatuto de veterano informaes de sade por exemplo para acomodar qualquer deficincia que o utilizador possa ter ou restries alimentares informaes relativas s opinies polticas ou crenas religiosas ou filiao sindical de uma pessoa informaes sobre as infraces ou condenaes criminais de um indivduo bem como quaisquer outras informaes consideradas sensveis ao abrigo das leis de proteo de dados aplicveis sempre que permitido por lei e na medida do aplicvel a honeywell poder tambm ter de efetuar verificaes de antecedentes eou criminais para determinar a sua adequao a um cargo ou oportunidade em aberto na honeywell no exigimos que o utilizador nos fornea informaes pessoais sensveis a menos que tal seja necessrio para efeitos de cumprimento das nossas obrigaes regulamentares por exemplo para controlo da igualdade de oportunidades ou que o utilizador tenha dado o seu consentimento explcito exceto na medida em que tal seja exigido por lei o fornecimento destas informaes ser totalmente voluntrio a honeywell est empenhada numa fora de trabalho verdadeiramente inclusiva e diversificada ao fornecernos os seus dados sobre igualdade de oportunidades permitenos compreender melhor o perfil dos nossos funcionrios em termos de dados sobre igualdade de oportunidades e as medidas que temos de tomar para atrair promover e manter uma fora de trabalho diversificada independentemente da idade deficincia sexo raa crenas religiosas ou filosficas e orientao sexual iii informaes pessoais que recolhemos automaticamente do utilizador podemos recolher automaticamente determinadas informaes sobre a sua visita aos nossos stios web utilizando cookies e outras tecnologias de rastreio semelhantes para mais informaes sobre os cookies que utilizamos no stio web atravs do qual apresenta a sua candidatura leia o nosso aviso sobre cookies fontes de informaes pessoais podemos recolher as suas informaes pessoais diretamente junto do utilizador ou indiretamente junto de terceiros que estejam legalmente autorizados a partilhar as suas informaes connosco tais como agncias de emprego prestadores de servios de verificao de antecedentesemprego ou de verificao de identidade agncias de recrutamento por exemplo quando uma agncia de recrutamento o identifica como potencial candidato informaes publicamente disponveis sobre si em stios como o linkedin ou o stio web do seu atual empregador o utilizador poder tambm optar por nos fornecer acesso a determinadas informaes pessoais armazenadas por terceiros por exemplo linkedin twitter google ou facebook ao autorizar a honeywell a ter acesso a estas informaes o utilizador concorda que podemos recolher armazenar e utilizar estas informaes de acordo com o presente aviso de privacidade por referncia ou boca a boca por exemplo atravs de uma referncia de um funcionrio atual ou antigo no caso de referncias a pessoa que o est a referir ser responsvel por obter o seu consentimento para nos fornecer as suas informaes pessoais finalidades para as quais as informaes pessoais so utilizadas utilizamos as suas informaes pessoais para os seguintes fins para avaliar a sua candidatura e tomar decises de contratao comunicar com o candidato e informlo sobre o recrutamento eou as suas candidaturas ou quaisquer outras comunicaes necessrias cumprir os requisitos legais e regulamentares aplicveis e para que possamos estabelecer exercer ou defender uma ao judicial emprego e gesto de empresas por exemplo estabelecer um registo de emprego bsico se for contratado elaborar relatriosanlises agregados sobre os dados de atividade dos candidatos por exemplo trfego do stio de carreiras funil de candidatos fonte de contratao sucesso da campanha de recrutamento apenas para funcionrios da honeywell para o excluir automaticamente de ser sugerido proactivamente para considerao aos recrutadores para uma oportunidade de emprego e no elegvel para considerao de acordo com a sua atual classificao hpd de 9 blocos que nunca ser revelada a ningum fora da honeywell no entanto poder sempre candidatarse diretamente a qualquer oportunidade de emprego disponvel e a sua situao especfica ser considerada por um recrutador apenas se o utilizador for residente nos estados unidos para lhe enviar comunicaes por sms especificamente i 11 comunicaes sms relacionadas com a sua candidatura a uma determinada vaga de emprego eou ii mediante o seu consentimento expresso comunicaes de campanhas considerm c dezvluirea este necesar n conformitate cu legislaia aplicabil sau n cazul n care credem cu bun credin c o astfel de aciune este necesar pentru a ne exercita stabili sau apra drepturile legale sau pentru a v proteja interesele vitale sau pe cele ale unei alte persoane de asemenea este posibil s mprtim informaiile dvs personale cu alte persoane cu consimmntul dvs sau la indicaiile dvs de exemplu un arbitru sau o asociaie profesional transferurile internaionale de informaii personale honeywell este o organizaie global iar informaiile dvs personale pot fi transferate pstrate stocate sau utilizate n diverse locaii din ntreaga lume cum ar fi sua i india acest lucru nseamn c atunci cnd colectm informaiile dvs personale acestea pot fi procesate n ri care pot avea legi privind protecia datelor diferite de legile din ara dvs cu toate acestea honeywell va lua ntotdeauna msuri rezonabile pentru a v proteja confidenialitatea i pentru a oferi un nivel de protecie a informaiilor personale comparabil cu cel din ara dumneavoastr de reedin printre care se numr punerea n aplicare a clauzelor contractuale standard ale comisiei europene care pot fi gsite pe siteul web al comisiei la candidai n mod similar n cazul n care am colectat i prelucrat informaiile dvs personale cu consimmntul dvs atunci v putei retrage consimmntul n orice moment retragerea consimmntului dvs nu va este aviso de privacidad del solicitante aviso de privacidad describe cmo honeywell international inc y sus filiales colectivamente honeywell nosotros procesan su informacin personal cuando usted se une a nuestra comunidad de talentos busca o solicita un empleo y nos enva informacin personal a travs de nuestro portal sitios web u otros medios de contratacin ya sea en lnea o fuera de lnea los servicios somos los responsables del tratamiento de su informacin personal a efectos de la legislacin aplicable en materia de proteccin de datos tenga en cuenta que si ya es empleado de honeywell tambin puede consultar la poltica global de privacidad de datos de honeywell y el aviso de privacidad para empleados en caso de que exista uno para su jurisdiccin el objetivo de este aviso de privacidad es proporcionarle informacin ms detallada sobre nuestro procesamiento de su informacin personal en relacin con su solicitud informacin personal que recopilamos para procesar su solicitud le pedimos que proporcione informacin personal sobre usted por ejemplo cuando se postula para una vacante en particular a travs de nuestro sitio webportal o en caso de que ya sea empleado de honeywell durante su relacin laboral toda la informacin se proporciona de forma voluntaria y usted determina el alcance de la informacin que proporciona a honeywell tenga en cuenta que algunos datos pueden ser necesarios para completar la evaluacin de su solicitud y que si no los facilita nuestra capacidad para considerarle candidato puede verse limitada i informacin personal podemos recopilar la siguiente informacin personal sobre usted datos personales e informacin de contacto como direccin de correo electrnico nmeros de telfono y fotografa informacin profesional y educativa relacionada con su ocupacin como sus empleadores actuales o anteriores su cargo u otra informacin sobre la organizacin a la que est afiliado tambin puede facilitar su currculum vtae e informacin sobre sus cualificaciones o su formacin como ttulos campos de estudio instituciones a las que ha asistido idiomas afiliaciones profesionales certificaciones detalles sobre las calificaciones de la gestin del rendimiento y la remuneracin preferencias profesionales por ejemplo objetivos a corto y largo plazo disposicin a trasladarse fecha disponible para trasladarse y preferencias de ubicacin datos personales derivados de su participacin en nuestro proceso de contratacin como por ejemplo los obtenidos durante las entrevistas los correos electrnicos que intercambiamos con usted en relacin con su solicitud o las conversaciones que mantenemos con usted a travs de nuestro chatbot en lnea informacin sonora y visual como su voz e imagen captadas en fotografas grabaciones de vdeo o audio si participa en una entrevista telefnica o de vdeo o si visita nuestras oficinas cualquier otra informacin personal que decida proporcionarnos voluntariamente ii informacin personal sensible tambin podemos recopilar categoras especiales de informacin personal sobre usted tambin conocidas como categoras especiales de informacin personal cuando tengamos la obligacin legal de hacerlo o lala informacin es relevante para su futuro entorno de trabajo en honeywell o para la futura provisin de beneficios laborales o con su consentimiento explcito como por ejemplo nmero de identificacin emitido por el gobierno como el nmero de la seguridad social informacin demogrfica que puede incluir informacin sobre clasificaciones protegidas como su edad sexo raza discapacidad orientacin sexual estado civil o condicin de veterano informacin sanitaria por ejemplo para adaptarse a cualquier discapacidad que pueda tener o a restricciones dietticas informacin relativa a las opiniones polticas creencias religiosas o afiliacin sindical de una persona informacin sobre delitos o condenas penales de un individuo as como cualquier otra informacin considerada sensible segn las leyes de proteccin de datos aplicables cuando la ley lo permita y en la medida en que corresponda honeywell tambin puede necesitar realizar verificaciones de antecedentes yo penales para determinar su idoneidad para un puesto vacante u oportunidad en honeywell no le pedimos que nos proporcione informacin personal sensible a menos que sea necesario para cumplir nuestras obligaciones reglamentarias por ejemplo para el control de la igualdad de oportunidades o a menos que nos haya dado su consentimiento explcito excepto en la medida en que lo exija la ley el suministro de esta informacin ser totalmente voluntario honeywell est comprometida con una verdadera fuerza laboral inclusiva y diversa al proporcionarnos sus datos de igualdad de oportunidades nos permite comprender mejor el perfil de nuestros empleados en trminos de datos de igualdad de oportunidades y las medidas que debemos tomar para atraer promover y retener una fuerza laboral diversa independientemente de la edad discapacidad sexo raza creencias religiosas o filosficas y orientacin sexual iii informacin personal que recopilamos automticamente de usted podemos recopilar automticamente cierta informacin sobre su visita a nuestros sitios web utilizando cookies y otras tecnologas de seguimiento similares para ms informacin sobre las cookies que utilizamos en el sitio web a travs del cual presenta su solicitud lea nuestro aviso sobre cookies fuentes de informacin personal podemos recabar sus datos personales directamente de usted o indirectamente de terceros que estn legalmente autorizados a compartir su informacin con informacin personal almacenada por terceros por ejemplo linkedin twitter google o facebook al autorizar a honeywell a tener acceso a esta informacin usted acepta que podamos recopilar almacenar y utilizar esta informacin de acuerdo con este aviso de privacidad por referencia o de boca en boca por ejemplo a travs de una recomendacin de un empleado actual o anterior en el caso de las referencias la persona que le recomiende ser responsable de obtener su consentimiento para facilitarnos sus datos personales fines para los que se utilizan los datos personales utilizamos su informacin personal para los siguientes fines para evaluar su solicitud y tomar decisiones de contratacin comunicarnos con usted e informarle sobre la contratacin yo sus candidaturas o cualquier otra comunicacin necesaria cumplir con los requisitos legales y reglamentarios aplicables y para que podamos establecer ejercer o defender una reclamacin legal empleo y gestin empresarial por ejemplo establecer un historial laboral bsico si se le contrata realizar informesanlisis agregados relativos a los datos de actividad de los candidatos por ejemplo trfico del sitio de empleo embudo de candidatos fuente de contratacin xito de la campaa de contratacin slo para empleados de honeywell para excluirlo automticamente de ser sugerido proactivamente para consideracin de los reclutadores para una oportunidad de ofrece y acepta un empleo en honeywell la informacin recopilada durante el proceso de solicitud y contratacin formar parte de su registro de empleo tratamiento automatizado y elaboracin de perfiles sujeto a su consentimiento expreso que usted proporciona voluntariamente al unirse a nuestra comunidad de talentos o al marcar la casilla de consentimiento correspondiente durante el proceso de solicitud realizamos perfiles para evaluar su idoneidad para determinadas oportunidades de empleo esto implica el uso de un algoritmo de comparacin capaz de evaluar su perfil laboral y predecir su idoneidad para una determinada oportunidad de empleo llevamos a cabo este tratamiento automatizado con los siguientes fines ayudar a los responsables de la seleccin de personal a adecuar los perfiles de los candidatos a las oportunidades de empleo sugiriendo candidatos a tener en cuenta para una oportunidad de empleo concreta y enviarle recomendaciones de trabajo personalizadas basadas en su perfil yo preferencias u otra informacin que pueda ser de su inters como noticias seminarios web y eventos de honeywell tenga en cuenta que sobre la base de este perfil es posible que no se le tenga en cuenta para determinadas oportunidades de empleo a menos que las haya solicitado directamente no tomamos decisiones de contratacin basadas nicamente en procesos automatizados de toma de decisiones yo elaboracin de perfiles sus datos personales se sometern a decisiones humanas ya que la decisin final de contratacin la tomarn los responsables de contratacin bases jurdicas del tratamiento de sus aradnzda veya bavurduunuzda ve portalmz web sitelerimiz veya dier ie alm ortamlar araclyla evrimii veya evrimd olarak kiisel bilgilerinizi bize gnderdiinizde hizmetler kiisel bilgilerinizi nasl ilediini aklamaktadr geerli veri koruma yasalarnn amalar dorultusunda kiisel bilgilerinizin kontrolrleri biziz halihazrda bir honeywell alanysanz honeywell global veri gizlilii politikasna ve yarg alannz iin varsa alan gizlilii bildirimine de bavurabileceinizi ltfen unutmayn bu gizlilik bildiriminin amac bavurunuzla ilgili olarak kiisel bilgilerinizi ilememiz hakknda size daha ayrntl bilgi vermektir topladmz kiisel bilgiler bavurunuzu ileme koymak iin rnein web sitemizportalmz araclyla belirli bir i ilanna bavurduunuzda veya halihazrda bir honeywell alan olmanz durumunda istihdam ilikiniz srasnda kendinizle ilgili kiisel bilgileri salamanz isteriz tm bilgiler gnlllk esasna gre salanr ve honeywelle verdiiniz bilgilerin kapsamn siz belirlersiniz bavurunuzun deerlendirilmesini tamamlamak iin baz bilgilerin gerekli olabileceini ve bu bilgilerin salanmamas halinde sizi aday olarak deerlendirme imkanmzn snrl olabileceini ltfen unutmayn i kiisel bilgiler sizin hakknzda aadaki kiisel bilgileri toplayabiliriz eposta adresi telefon numarasnumaralar ve fotoraf dahil olmak zere kiisel bilgiler ve iletiim bilgileri mevcut veya nceki iverenleriniz i unvannz veya bal olduunuz english updated 1 january 2023 this applicant privacy notice privacy notice describes how honeywell international inc and its affiliates collectively honeywell us or we process your personal information when you join our talent community search or apply for a job and submit personal information to us via our portal websites or other recruitment mediums whether online or offline the services we are the controllers of your personal information for the purposes of applicable data protection laws please note that if you are already a honeywell employee you can also refer to the honeywell global data privacy policy and the employee privacy notice where one exists for your jurisdiction the aim of this privacy notice is to give you more detailed information about our processing of your personal information in relation to your application personal information we collect to process your application we ask you to provide the personal information about yourself for example when you apply for a particular job vacancy through our websiteportal or in case that you already are a honeywell employee during your employment relationship all information is provided on a voluntary basis and you determine the extent of information you provide to honeywell please bear in mind that some information may be necessary to complete an evaluation of your application and if it is not provided our ability to consider you as a candidate may be limited i personal information we may collect the following personal information about you personal details and contact information including email address telephone numbers and photograph professional and educational information related to your occupation such as your current or previous employers your job title or other information about the organization with which you are affiliated you may also provide your cvresume and information about your qualifications or your education such as your degrees fields of study the institutions youve attended languages professional memberships certifications details on performance management ratings and compensation career preferences eg shortterm and longterm goals willingness to relocate date available to relocate and location preferences personal information derived from your participation in our recruitment process such as for example those obtained during interviews the emails we exchange with you regarding your application or the conversations we have with you through our online chatbot audio and visual information such as your voice and likeness as captured in photographs video or audio recordings if you participate in a phone or video interview or if you visit our offices any other personal information that you voluntarily choose to provide to us ii sensitive personal information we may also collect special categories of personal information about you also known as special categories of personal information where we have a legal obligation to do so or the information is relevant to your future working environment at honeywell or for the future provision of employment benefits or with your explicit consent such as governmentissued identification number such as a social security number demographic information which may include information about protected classifications such as your age gender race disabilities sexual orientation marital status or veteran status health information for example to accommodate any disability you may have or dietary restrictions information relating to a persons political opinions or religious beliefs or trade union membership information about an individuals criminal offences or convictions as well as any other information deemed sensitive under applicable data protection laws where permitted by law and to the extent applicable honeywell may also need to carry out background andor criminal checks to determine your suitability for an open position or opportunity at honeywell we do not require you to provide us with sensitive personal information unless it is necessary for the purposes of carrying out our regulatory obligations eg for equal opportunity monitoring or unless you have provided your explicit consent except to the extent required by law the provision of this information will be entirely voluntary honeywell is committed to a true inclusive and diverse workforce by providing us with your equal opportunity data you allow us to better understand our employee profile in terms of equal opportunities data and the action we need to take to attract promote and retain a diverse workforce regardless of age disability gender race religious or philosophical beliefs and sexual orientation iii personal information we collect automatically from you we may automatically collect certain information from you about your visit to our websites using cookies and other similar tracking technologies for further information about the cookies we use on the website through which you submit your application please read our cookie notice sources of personal information we may collect your personal information directly from you or indirectly from third parties who are lawfully entitled to share your information with us such as employment agencies backgroundemployment check or identity verification service providers recruitment agencies for example when a recruitment agency identifies you as a potential candidate publicly available information about you from sites such as linkedin or your current employers website you may also choose to provide us with access to certain personal information stored by third parties for example linkedin twitter google or facebook by authorizing honeywell to have access to this information you agree that we may collect store and use this information in accordance with this privacy notice by reference or word of mouth for example through a referral from a current or former employee for referrals the person who is referring you will be responsible for obtaining your consent to provide us with your personal information purposes for which personal information is used we use your personal information for the following purposes to evaluate your application and make hiring decisions communicate with you and to inform you about the recruitment andor your applications or any other required communications comply with applicable legal and regulatory requirements and in order for us to establish exercise or defend a legal claim employment and corporate management for example establish a basic employment record if you are hired to carry out aggregated reports analysis regarding candidates activity data eg career site traffic candidate funnel source of hire recruiting campaign success for honeywell employees only to automatically exclude you from being proactively suggested for consideration to recruiters for a job opportunity and are not eligible for consideration per your current hpd 9block rating which will never be revealed to anyone outside honeywell however you will always be able to directly apply for any job opportunity available and your specific situation will be considered by a recruiter only where you are a resident of the united states to send you communications via sms specifically i 11 sms communications in connection with your application to a particular job vacancy andor ii subject to your express consent sms campaign communications about employment opportunities job affairs and application updates you will be able to opt out andor revoke your consent for receiving the abovementioned communications following the instructions given in your profile if you are offered and accept employment with honeywell the information collected during the application and recruitment process will become part of your employment record automated processing and profiling subject to your express consent which you voluntarily provide when joining our talent community or when checking the appropriate consent box during the application process we conduct profiling to evaluate your suitability for particular job opportunities this involves using a matching algorithm that is able to evaluate your employment profile and predict your eligibility for a particular job opportunity we carry out this automated processing for the purposes of helping recruiters match candidates profiles to job opportunities by suggesting candidates for consideration for a specific job opportunity and sending personalized job recommendations to you based on your profile andor preferences or other information that may be of interest for you such as honeywell news webinars and events please note that based on this profiling you may not be considered for certain job opportunities unless you have applied for them directly we do not make hiring decisions based solely on automated decisionmaking processes andor profiling your personal information will be subjected to humanmade decisions as the ultimate hiring decision will be made by the recruiters or hiring manager the legal bases for processing your personal information certain jurisdictions require honeywell to have a legal basis for processing your personal information where applicable law requires us to justify our processing activities our legal basis for collecting and using your personal information as described in this privacy notice will depend on the personal information concerned and the specific context in which we collect it consent in general we will normally collect personal information from you where we have your consent to do so and where we need your personal information to process your application by accessing our websiteportal joining our talent community or applying for one of our job positions you provide your consent to honeywell to collect and further process the personal information described above for the purposes described in this privacy notice you may withdraw your consent at any time by professional association international transfers of personal information honeywell is a global organization and your personal information may be transferred to held stored or used across various locations worldwide such as the us and india this means that when we collect your personal information it may be processed in countries that may have data protection laws that are different to the laws of your country however honeywell will always take reasonable steps to protect your privacy and to provide a level of protection of personal information that is comparable to that of your country of residence which include implementing the european commissions standard contractual clauses which may be found at the commissions website at httpseceuropaeu retention we will retain your personal information for as long as necessary in connection with the purposes described in this privacy notice and in accordance with honeywells record retention schedule or as required by applicable law your residents below you may have the right to access correct update or request deletion of your personal information you can object to the processing of your personal information ask us to restrict processing of your personal information or request portability of your personal information you may have the right not to have a decision made about you that is based solely on automated processing including profiling if that decision produces legal effects about you or significantly affects you honeywell does not as part of its recruitment process make solely automated decisions about candidates similarly if we have collected and process your personal information with your consent then you can withdraw your consent at any time withdrawing your consent will not affect the lawfulness of any processing we conducted prior to your withdrawal nor will it affect processing of your personal information conducted in reliance on lawful processing grounds other than consent and you have httpswwwhoneywellcomenusprivacystatement norwegian oppdatert 1 januar 2023 denne personvernerklringen for skere personvernerklringen beskriver hvordan honeywell international inc og dets tilknyttede selskaper samlet kalt honeywell oss eller vi behandler personopplysningene dine nr du blir medlem av talent community sker eller sker p en jobb og sender inn personopplysninger til oss via vr portal vre nettsteder eller andre rekrutteringsmedier enten online eller offline tjenestene vi er behandlingsansvarlige for personopplysningene dine i henhold til gjeldende personvernlovgivning vr oppmerksom p at hvis du allerede er ansatt hos honeywell kan du ogs lese honeywells globale retningslinjer for personvern og personvernerklringen for ansatte der det finnes en slik for din jurisdiksjon formlet sknaden din ber vi deg om oppgi personopplysninger om deg selv for eksempel nr du sker p en bestemt ledig stilling via nettstedetportalen vr eller hvis du allerede er ansatt hos honeywell i lpet av ditt ansettelsesforhold all informasjon gis p frivillig basis og du bestemmer selv hvor mye informasjon du gir til honeywell vr oppmerksom p at enkelte opplysninger kan vre ndvendige for kunne vurdere sknaden din og hvis du ikke oppgir disse kan det begrense vr mulighet til vurdere deg som kandidat i personlig informasjon vi kan samle inn flgende personopplysninger om deg personopplysninger og faglige medlemskap sertifiseringer informasjon om prestasjonsvurderinger og kompensasjon karrierepreferanser feks kortsiktige og langsiktige ml vilje til flytte dato for flytting og stedspreferanser enero de 2023 este aviso de privacidad del solicitante aviso de privacidad describe cmo honeywell international inc y sus filiales colectivamente honeywell nosotros procesan su informacin personal cuando usted se une a nuestra comunidad de talentos busca o solicita un empleo y nos enva informacin personal a travs de nuestro portal sitios web u otros medios de contratacin ya sea en lnea o fuera de lnea los servicios somos los responsables del tratamiento de su informacin personal a efectos de la legislacin aplicable en materia de proteccin de datos tenga en cuenta que si ya es empleado de honeywell tambin puede consultar la poltica global de privacidad de datos de honeywell y el aviso de privacidad para empleados en caso de que exista uno para su jurisdiccin el objetivo de este aviso de privacidad es proporcionarle informacin ms detallada sobre nuestro procesamiento de su informacin personal en relacin con su solicitud informacin personal que recopilamos para procesar su solicitud le pedimos que proporcione informacin personal sobre usted por ejemplo cuando se postula para una vacante en particular a travs de nuestro sitio webportal o en caso de que ya sea empleado de honeywell durante su relacin laboral toda la informacin se proporciona de forma voluntaria y usted determina el alcance de la informacin que proporciona a honeywell tenga en cuenta que algunos datos pueden ser necesarios para completar la evaluacin de su solicitud y que si no los facilita nuestra capacidad para considerarle candidato puede verse limitada i informacin personal podemos recopilar la siguiente informacin personal sobre usted datos personales e informacin de contacto como direccin de correo electrnico nmeros de telfono y fotografa informacin profesional y educativa relacionada con su ocupacin como sus empleadores actuales o anteriores su cargo u otra informacin sobre la organizacin a la que est afiliado tambin puede facilitar su currculum vtae e informacin sobre sus cualificaciones o su formacin como ttulos campos de estudio instituciones a las que ha asistido idiomas afiliaciones profesionales certificaciones detalles sobre las calificaciones de la gestin del rendimiento y la remuneracin preferencias profesionales por ejemplo objetivos a corto y largo plazo disposicin a trasladarse fecha disponible para trasladarse y preferencias de ubicacin datos personales derivados de su participacin en nuestro proceso de contratacin como por ejemplo los obtenidos durante las entrevistas los correos electrnicos que intercambiamos con usted en relacin con su solicitud o las conversaciones que mantenemos con usted a travs de nuestro chatbot en lnea informacin sonora y visual como su voz e imagen captadas en fotografas grabaciones de vdeo o audio si participa en una entrevista telefnica o de vdeo o si visita nuestras oficinas cualquier otra informacin personal que decida proporcionarnos voluntariamente ii informacin personal sensible tambin podemos recopilar categoras especiales de informacin personal sobre usted tambin conocidas como categoras especiales de informacin personal cuando tengamos la obligacin legal de hacerlo o lala informacin es relevante para su futuro entorno de trabajo en honeywell o para la futura provisin de beneficios laborales o con su consentimiento explcito como por ejemplo nmero de identificacin emitido por el gobierno como el nmero de la seguridad social informacin demogrfica que puede incluir informacin sobre clasificaciones protegidas como su edad sexo raza discapacidad orientacin sexual estado civil o condicin de veterano informacin sanitaria por ejemplo para adaptarse a cualquier discapacidad que pueda tener o a restricciones dietticas informacin relativa a las opiniones polticas creencias religiosas o afiliacin sindical de una persona informacin sobre delitos o condenas penales de un individuo as como cualquier otra informacin considerada sensible segn las leyes de proteccin de datos aplicables cuando la ley lo permita y en la medida en que corresponda honeywell tambin puede necesitar realizar verificaciones de antecedentes yo penales para determinar su idoneidad para un puesto vacante u oportunidad en honeywell no le pedimos que nos proporcione informacin personal sensible a menos que sea necesario para cumplir nuestras obligaciones reglamentarias por ejemplo para el control de la igualdad de oportunidades o a menos que nos haya dado su consentimiento explcito excepto en la medida en que lo exija la ley el suministro de esta informacin ser totalmente voluntario honeywell est comprometida con una verdadera fuerza laboral inclusiva y diversa al proporcionarnos sus datos de igualdad de oportunidades nos permite comprender mejor el perfil de nuestros empleados en trminos de datos de igualdad de oportunidades y las medidas que debemos tomar para atraer promover y retener una fuerza laboral diversa independientemente de la edad discapacidad sexo raza creencias religiosas o filosficas y orientacin sexual iii informacin personal que recopilamos automticamente de usted podemos recopilar automticamente cierta informacin sobre su visita a nuestros sitios web utilizando cookies y otras tecnologas de seguimiento similares para ms informacin sobre las cookies que utilizamos en el sitio web a travs del cual presenta su solicitud lea nuestro aviso sobre cookies fuentes de informacin personal podemos recabar sus datos personales directamente de usted o indirectamente de terceros que estn legalmente autorizados a compartir su informacin con nosotros como por ejemplo agencias de empleo proveedores de servicios de verificacin de antecedentesempleo o de identidad agencias de contratacin por ejemplo cuando una agencia de contratacin le identifica como posible candidato informacin pblica sobre usted procedente de sitios como linkedin o el sitio web de su empleador actual tambin puede optar por proporcionarnos acceso a cierta informacin personal almacenada por terceros por ejemplo linkedin twitter google o facebook al autorizar a honeywell a tener acceso a esta informacin usted acepta que podamos recopilar almacenar y utilizar esta informacin de acuerdo con este aviso de privacidad por referencia o de boca en boca por ejemplo a travs de una recomendacin de un empleado actual o anterior en el caso de las referencias la persona que le recomiende ser responsable de obtener su consentimiento para facilitarnos sus datos personales fines para los que se utilizan los datos personales utilizamos su informacin personal para los siguientes fines para evaluar su solicitud y tomar decisiones de contratacin comunicarnos con usted e informarle sobre la contratacin yo sus candidaturas o cualquier otra comunicacin necesaria cumplir con los requisitos legales y reglamentarios aplicables y para que podamos establecer ejercer o defender una reclamacin legal empleo y gestin empresarial por ejemplo establecer un historial laboral bsico si se le contrata realizar informesanlisis agregados relativos a los datos de actividad de los candidatos por ejemplo trfico del sitio de empleo embudo de candidatos fuente de contratacin xito de la campaa de contratacin slo para empleados de honeywell para excluirlo automticamente de ser sugerido proactivamente para consideracin de los reclutadores para una oportunidad de trabajo y no es elegible para consideracin por su calificacin actual de hpd de 9 bloques que nunca ser revelada a nadie fuera de honeywell sin embargo siempre podr solicitar directamente cualquier oportunidad de trabajo disponible y su situacin especfica ser considerada por un reclutador nicamente si reside en estados unidos para enviarle comunicaciones por sms en concreto i 11 comunicaciones por sms en relacin con su candidatura a una determinada oferta de empleo yo ii previo consentimiento expreso por su parte comunicaciones de campaas por sms sobre oportunidades de empleo asuntos laborales y actualizaciones de solicitudes podr darse de baja yo revocar su consentimiento para recibir las comunicaciones mencionadas siguiendo las instrucciones que figuran en su perfil si se le ofrece y acepta un empleo en honeywell la informacin recopilada durante el proceso de solicitud y contratacin formar parte de su registro de empleo tratamiento automatizado y elaboracin de perfiles sujeto a su consentimiento expreso que usted proporciona voluntariamente al unirse a nuestra comunidad de talentos o al marcar la casilla de consentimiento correspondiente durante el proceso de solicitud realizamos perfiles para evaluar su idoneidad para determinadas oportunidades de empleo esto implica el uso de un algoritmo de comparacin capaz de evaluar su perfil laboral y predecir su idoneidad para una determinada oportunidad de empleo llevamos a cabo este tratamiento automatizado con los siguientes fines ayudar a los responsables de la seleccin de personal a adecuar los perfiles de los candidatos a las oportunidades de empleo sugiriendo candidatos a tener en cuenta para una oportunidad de empleo concreta y enviarle recomendaciones de trabajo personalizadas basadas en su perfil yo preferencias u otra informacin que pueda ser de su inters como noticias seminarios web y eventos de honeywell tenga en cuenta que sobre la base de este perfil es posible que no se le tenga en cuenta para determinadas oportunidades de empleo a menos que las haya solicitado directamente no tomamos decisiones de contratacin basadas nicamente en procesos automatizados de toma de decisiones yo elaboracin de perfiles sus datos personales se sometern a decisiones humanas ya que la decisin final de contratacin la tomarn los responsables de contratacin bases jurdicas del tratamiento de sus datos personales ciertas jurisdicciones exigen que honeywell tenga una base legal para procesar su informacin personal cuando la legislacin aplicable nos exija justificar nuestras actividades de procesamiento nuestra base legal para recopilar y utilizar su informacin personal segn se describe en este aviso de privacidad depender de la informacin personal en cuestin y del contexto especfico en recopilar y procesar la informacin personal descrita anteriormente para los fines descritos en este aviso de privacidad puede retirar su consentimiento en cualquier momento enviando una solicitud a intereses vitales o los de otra persona tambin podemos compartir su informacin personal con terceros con su consentimiento o por indicacin suya por ejemplo un rbitro o una asociacin profesional transferencias internacionales de datos personales hhoneywell es una organizacin global y su informacin personal puede transferirse guardarse almacenarse o utilizarse en varios lugares del mundo como eeuu e india esto significa que cuando recopilamos su informacin personal sta puede ser procesada en pases que pueden tener leyes de proteccin de datos diferentes a las leyes de su pas sin embargo implementacin de las clusulas contractuales tipo de la comisin europea que se pueden encontrar en el sitio web de la comisin en httpseceuropaeu retencin conservaremos su informacin personal durante el honeywell alanlar zaten bir honeywell alanysanz profilinizdeki baz blmlerin herkese ak olduunu ve bu nedenle tm honeywell alanlar tarafndan grlebileceini ltfen unutmayn zellikle adnz unvannz fotorafnz becerileriniz ilgi alanlarnz i deneyiminiz ve eitiminiz ancak bu blmler dzenlenebilir ve profilinizde sizinle ilgili hangi bilgilerin gsterileceini seebileceksiniz ltfen kariyer hedeflerinin yer deitirmelerin ve profil durumu yeni frsatlara ak blmleri herkese ak olmayacak ve bu nedenle tm honeywell alanlar tarafndan grlemeyecektir yalnzca honeywellin yetenek ekibi tarafndan dier nc taraflar honeywell ifann yrrlkteki yasalar uyarnca gerekli olduuna inandmz veya yasal haklarmz kullanmak tesis etmek veya savunmak ya da sizin veya baka bir kiinin hayati karlarn korumak iin bu tr bir eylemin izninizle veya sizin talimatnzla bakalaryla da paylaabiliriz rnein bir hakem veya meslek birlii kiisel bilgilerin uluslararas aktarm honeywell kresel bir kurulutur ve kiisel bilgileriniz abd ve hindistan gibi dnya apnda eitli konumlara aktarlabilir tutulabilir saklanabilir veya kullanlabilir bu kiisel bilgilerinizi topladmzda lkenizin yasalarndan farkl veri koruma yasalarna sahip olabilecek
